## Text Elements
generative process (different orderings possible)

A. sample biological entity - e.g. cell)
B. sample perspective (genes) - source of biological signal
C. sample representation (batch effect: method, site, donor, batch) ^GP6WCeyY

hyper prior over (Z_A, Z_BC) ^COwSn4Mm

samples from
all components ^UWxZf7Wd

captures uncertainty related with BC ^B1Vivow9

PRIOR CONDITIONING MODEL
- INPUT:
    - bag of condition tokens
    - just biological conditions: e.g. celltype, pathology
- OUTPUT:
    - GM prior on Z_A
- CONDITION TOKEN EMBEDDINGS
    1) condition known
        a) present -> present TOKEN
        b) absent  -> absent TOKEN
        c) magnitude -> magnitude modified TOKEN ( e.g. +/concat sthg)
    2) condition unknown
        - ??? ^L9MDGYP9

ideally ^94x3TxvJ

we may do further
processing
before obtaining Z_A ^UKXCZEsP

simple prior like N(0, I) we let the posteriors learn
the generative process on its own and model the uncertainty
related with BC using GM of
    - e.g. 250 components
    ~ the complexity of the posterioris a function of the uncertainty bound to a specific sample -> different no of components (thresholding, stick-breaking)
        - PROBLEM??? - differing no of reconstructed samples between cells ^4ps79kND

mean weighted by components probability
    -> we learn the component logits
or
logsumex of the total loss for each sample
    -> do we learn the component logits?
        are they used in weighting? ^4VmJUohP

    - ... requires  ^DaQ3tcUg
